The operating time of the shuttle bus from the hotel to the scenic spot is from 9:00 to 21:00 in the morning. If you want to go to the yard early in the morning, you need to make a reservation with the lady at the front desk about 20 minutes in advance. This trip was very good, and I will come again next time .

There is no reason, intuition. Facts have proved that a man's sixth sense is quite accurate, especially the wind-like Aquarius ‚ôíÔ∏è.

What age is it, and I still want to make more money by detouring tricks, there is really no technical content.

All the way to the entrance of the Zen town of Nianhuawan, they were stopped by security and asked to buy a ticket. In fact, if you buy it one day in advance, there will be a discount for the public, and the package ticket between the town and the Lingshan Buddha is only 258, and the homework is not done. Compared with the room rate, the money is not much, but it feels uncomfortable to be bundled. The driver chirped and said that he used to be delivered to the gate of the scenic spot. The taxi driver in Wuxi left a bad impression on me.

A white lotus in full bloom in the hall welcomes visitors from all directions, politely. There is a distributor conference of a Fortune 500 multinational company that has reserved the venue, and a group of employees dressed in white "Victory" tee make the hotel more popular.

The deluxe suites on the executive floor are very large, with ample living room, bedroom and bathroom space, and the terrace is about 30 to 40 square meters. The hotel located in the mountains and forests is very quiet, the vegetation outside the window is lush, and the sounds of people are not heard, only the sound of birds.

After simple cleaning, we went to the restaurant on the 6th floor to enjoy the afternoon tea provided by the suite. It's very clean, and we booked the venue for almost two days. The self-service afternoon tea is quite rich in variety, including snacks, fruits, and drinks. From 5:00 to 7:00 to happy hour, there are fried chicken, burgers, sushi, and Yangzhou fried rice. If you are not so picky, it will be no problem for dinner. Anyway, we did not eat dinner properly for two days. Of course, there are also high-quality human men who have raised questions. A gentleman came in and turned around and said to the waiter, "I have stayed in hotels all over the world. Your meal is too shabby, you can't eat it at all." He turned and left. The waiter sister listened with a smile, and we sighed that the gap between people is still quite large.

The little girl who seemed to be about 20 years old was very gentle and thoughtful. She took the initiative to clean up the dinner plates, introduce us to the hotel and scenic spots, and ask us our opinions on hotel facilities and services. The little girl who knows how to interact positively with guests has a bright future.

On the 6th floor restaurant directly opposite the terrace behind the workbench is an egg, where you can take a panoramic view of the hotel, and you can see the beautiful sunset of Taihu Lake. From the perspective of the architectural layout and the exterior, it looks like Fujian Tulou and Banyan Tree Shuhe; from the interior decoration, I think of Mandarin Oriental Taipei, especially the large elevator. This Secret Realm is exactly what he recommended.

The hotel is located in the small town scenic area, only a five-minute walk away from Smile Square, one of the main attractions. But the evening breeze is really intoxicating, the night is really charming, and a walk is even more wonderful.
Both nights we ordered takeaway back to the room supper at the same store. Garlic flower beetles, garlic mushrooms, roast beef skewers, paired with the Paris water provided by the hotel, are more suitable for me than drinking beer. Soak in the bathtub before going to bed. Guests on the executive floor could have gone to the restaurant on the 6th floor. A buffet for breakfast and a buffet for afternoon tea is really enough for one day.
